NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
M. Mohammed Yakub a Male Child born to S. Meeranaina on 14th April 1987. I residing at No. 69/33, Saja
Munnusamy Street, Old Washermenpet, Chennai-600 021. Has been living as a Female after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. Jayaraman, Professor and Head Department of burns Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk
Medical College & hospital, Chennai-600 010. Reg No. 32070. By this I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth
be known as M. SHAINABANU.
Chennai, 28th August 2014.

M. MOHAMMED YAKUB.

CANCELLATION OF ADOPTION
I, adopted S. Sharmila, daughter of Thiru S. Udayakumar & Tmt. V. Kavitha born on 12th May 2007
(native district Cuddalore), residing at No. 25-C, 408 Quarters, Neyveli after executing an adoption deed on 27th May 2007
as I did not have a child then and named her as S. Sanjana Shivavani, which was published in Tamil Nadu
Government Gazette Part VI-4 Issue No. 42, dated 31st October 2007 at Page No. 1350. But now, as I have two children
of my own. We decided to cancel the adoption deed mutually and through II Additional Subordinate Judge, Cuddalore Court
Order (O.S. No. 65/2013) we got the above adoption cancelled. By this, S. Sanjana Shivani can now assume her old name
and shall be called as S. SHARMILA.
Neyveli,
28th August 2014.

K. SARAVANAKUMAR.
(Foster Parent.)
